Job Type: Full-Time

Job Description:
We are seeking a dedicated and detail-oriented Legal Support Worker to join our dynamic legal team. The ideal candidate will have a background in public relations and strong problem-solving skills. This role supports our attorneys and ensures the smooth operation of legal processes.

Responsibilities:
- Assist attorneys with case management and documentation.
- Perform legal research and draft correspondence.
- Manage client communications and maintain confidentiality.
- Coordinate schedules and meetings.
- Organize and maintain legal files and records.

Qualifications and Experience:

- Strong problem-solving and organizational skills.
- Excellent written and verbal communication skills.
- Proficiency in Microsoft Office Suite and legal research tools.

Perks and Benefits:
- Competitive salary ranging from 40,000 to 60,000 USD annually, based on experience and skills.
- Comprehensive health, dental, and vision insurance.
- Paid time off and holidays.
- Professional development opportunities.
- A supportive, inclusive work environment.

Application Process:
Interested candidates are encouraged to apply by submitting their resume and a cover letter detailing their qualifications and experience.

Equal Opportunity Employer:
Wilkins, Martin and Gallegos is committed to creating a diverse environment and is proud to be an equal opportunity employer. All qualified applicants will receive consideration for employment without regard to race, color, religion, gender, gender identity or expression, sexual orientation, national origin, genetics, disability, age, or veteran status.

We are seeking a qualified Procurement Specialist to join our team. This role is essential in ensuring our procurement processes are efficient, cost-effective, and align with our regulatory standards.

- Manage stakeholder relationships, including suppliers and internal departments.
- Ensure compliance with regulatory requirements and industry standards.

- Proficiency in project planning and management tools.

- Comprehensive health insurance including dental and vision.
- Generous paid time off and holiday schedule.
- Professional development opportunities.
- Flexible working arrangements, including remote work options.

Aguilar, Miller and Jones is an equal opportunity employer. We encourage individuals from diverse backgrounds to apply and join our inclusive team.

Company: Everett Group  
Role: Human Resources Associate

Company Background:
Everett Group is a leading global consulting firm dedicated to providing innovative solutions to complex business challenges. Our commitment to diversity and inclusion is reflected in our core principles, as we believe that diverse perspectives lead to innovative solutions.  

Job Type: Full-time

Job Description:
We are seeking a Human Resources Associate to join our team. The successful candidate will play a critical role in supporting various HR functions, including recruitment, onboarding, employee relations, and compliance. This role requires strong interpersonal skills and the ability to manage multiple projects simultaneously.  

Responsibilities:
- Assist in the recruitment and selection process, including posting job ads, screening resumes, and conducting interviews.
- Manage employee onboarding and orientation programs.
- Support employee relations activities and provide guidance on HR policies.
- Assist in the development and implementation of HR initiatives and systems.
- Ensure compliance with labor regulations.
- Maintain accurate employee records and manage HR documentation.

Qualifications and Experience:
- Bachelor’s degree in Human Resources, Business Administration, or a related field.
- At least 2 years of experience in human resources or a related field.
- Strong interpersonal and communication skills.
- Proficiency in project planning and time management.
- Knowledge of HR best practices and labor legislation.

Perks and Benefits:
- Competitive salary ranging from $50,000 to $70,000, based on experience and skills.
- Comprehensive health, dental, and vision insurance.
- Opportunities for professional development and career growth.
- Flexible work environment with the option to work remotely.
- Generous paid time off and holiday schedule.

Everett Group fosters an inclusive environment where everyone can thrive. We are committed to fair and equitable pay practices. Diversity and inclusion are core principles of our organization, and we encourage candidates from all backgrounds to apply.
